				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en" itemprop="name">Constellation</h1>				<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
					<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Grim Dawn Wiki</div>					<div id="contentSub"></div>
										<div id="jump-to-nav" class="mw-jump">
						Jump to:						<a href="#mw-head">navigation</a>, 						<a href="#p-search">search</a>
					</div>
					<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div class="floatright"><a href="/File:Crossroads_Constellation_Icon.png" class="image"><img alt="Crossroads Constellation Icon.png" src="https://gamepedia.cursecdn.com/grimdawn_gamepedia_en/thumb/7/77/Crossroads_Constellation_Icon.png/200px-Crossroads_Constellation_Icon.png?version=b3156f1668b2a0b26371aecbc1de76d3" width="200" height="203" class="thumbborder" srcset="https://gamepedia.cursecdn.com/grimdawn_gamepedia_en/thumb/7/77/Crossroads_Constellation_Icon.png/300px-Crossroads_Constellation_Icon.png?version=b3156f1668b2a0b26371aecbc1de76d3 1.5x, https://gamepedia.cursecdn.com/grimdawn_gamepedia_en/7/77/Crossroads_Constellation_Icon.png?version=b3156f1668b2a0b26371aecbc1de76d3 2x" /></a></div>
<p>There are a total of 82 Constellations, each made up of between 3 and 8 stars, which total 434. The <a href="/Ashes_of_Malmouth" title="Ashes of Malmouth">Ashes of Malmouth</a> Expansion adds another 14 Constellations.
</p><p>On gaining their first <a href="/Devotion" title="Devotion">Devotion</a> point, the player can choose one of the stars of the <a href="/Crossroads" title="Crossroads">Crossroads</a> constellation to spend it in. This grants an affinity point which unlocks other constellations. These in turn grant the Affinity required to unlock constellations of a higher level.
</p><p>Constellations are ranked in 3 main tiers, from center to  the edge of the Devotion window:
</p>
<ul><li>Tier 1 Constellations requires a single Affinity point and give a large Affinity bonus.</li>
<li>Tier 2 Constellations require between 8 and 11 Affinity and give a smaller Affinity bonus.</li>
<li>Tier 3 Constellations require 20+ Affinity and give no Affinity bonus.</li></ul>
<p>Note that Constellations are self-supporting, and their own Affinity bonus counts toward their Affinity requirement. Points can thus be re-allocated from other constellations used to reach them when their bonus is no longer required.
</p>
